posted:Posted April 9, 2024
msg:Looking out from the hotel lobby, there is a mirror-like lake view, with flowers and green trees on the water in the distance, and several black-sailed boats nearby. The combination of the distance and the near gives it a flavor of an ancient city. When checking in, because the weather suddenly warmed up, the gentleman at the front desk arranged a room on a high floor with a lake view and away from the sun. The room attendants were enthusiastic and made the turndown at night. When making the turndown, they would add paper towels + bottled drinking water, etc. according to the situation of the room; in the evening, the room would be given desserts, Tremella and peach gum soup, and the desserts were served in small bowls with covers, which was quite high-quality. The swimming pool has a suitable temperature, and the water is clean and refreshing without the smell of chlorine. The only small regret is that we communicated with the front desk the day before check-out and agreed that check-out could be delayed to 14:00 the next day. In fact, the front desk called at 13:00 to urge check-out, which affected the overall arrangement. There is room for improvement in the details of the front desk service.
